[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is a **heap-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation that accesses memory beyond the allocated buffer boundary. [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer has assigned this a scariness score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m, categorizing it as a [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the execution of the json_fuzz fuzzer with the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing characteristics:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Location of the overflow**: The invalid read occurs at address [0m[1;36m0x5020000000bd[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich is located exactly [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m13[0m[39m-byte memory region allocated at [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x5020000000b0[0m[39m.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call stack leading to the vulnerability**:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow originates in `json_parse_ex` function at [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m327:49[0m[39m`[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Called by `json_parse` at `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m958:11[0m[39m`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Invoked through the fuzzer harness `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` at [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/[0m[95mjson_fuzz.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m12:9[0m[39m`[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Executed by the LibFuzzer framework's callback mechanism[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory allocation details**: The [0m[1;36m13[0m[39m-byte buffer was allocated through the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstandard `malloc` function, triggered by the fuzzer's `RunOneTest` function during [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest case processing.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Shadow memory analysis**: The shadow byte representation shows the memory [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion with value `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m05[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` at the overflow location, indicating partial [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddressability [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m5[0m[39m out of [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes are valid in that memory word[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The surrounding [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory shows heap redzone markers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fa`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which are used by AddressSanitizer to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetect out-of-bounds accesses.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and the ASAN crash report, I've identified the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause of the heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause:** The JSON parser uses pre-increment operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`*++ state.ptr`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin boundary check conditions. The current boundary checks are off-by-one: they [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mverify there are N bytes remaining before performing N pre-increment operations, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut each `*++ state.ptr` increments the pointer FIRST, then dereferences it. This [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmeans N pre-increments will read from positions `state.ptr+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` through [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`state.ptr+N`, requiring N+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m bytes of space from the current position.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Finding:** The ASAN crash occurs at line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m in the surrogate pair handling [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode, which is NOT fixed by the provided good_patch.diff. The good patch only fixes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m, leaving four other vulnerable locations unpatched.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Identify All Vulnerable Boundary Checks[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThere are five locations in `src/json.c` with the same off-by-one error pattern:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m** - Unicode escape `\uXXXX` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Current: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fix: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Status: Already fixed in good_patch.diff[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m** - Unicode surrogate pair `\uXXXX\uYYYY` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbackslash + u + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Current: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fix: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Status: NOT FIXED - **This is where ASAN crashes**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m** - Keyword [0m[32m"true"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mr + u + e[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Current: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fix: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m** - Keyword [0m[32m"false"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma + l + s + e[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Current: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fix: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Status: NOT FIXED[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m** - Keyword [0m[32m"null"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mu + l + l[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Current: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Apply Boundary Check Corrections[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mStarting from the initial codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore any patches[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, apply the following [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges to `src/json.c`:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m - Line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUnicode escape[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Before:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || [0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m - Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSurrogate pair - PRIMARY FIX FOR ASAN CRASH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Before:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m[32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m[32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m - Line [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mKeyword [0m[32m"true"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Before:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'r'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'r'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m - Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mKeyword [0m[32m"false"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Before:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m - Line [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mKeyword [0m[32m"null"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Before:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Verification of Logic Preservation[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese changes are surgical and preserve all existing functionality:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Unicode Support**: The surrogate pair conversion logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m333[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m337[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged. Only the boundary check is corrected.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Two-Pass Parsing**: The fixes apply to both parsing passes since they only [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maffect boundary checks, not memory allocation or data processing.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Error Handling**: The same error messages and goto statements remain [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Escape Sequences**: All other escape sequence handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\b`, `\f`, `\n`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`\r`, `\t`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is unaffected.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **String Processing**: The UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m encoding logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m340[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m377[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains intact.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses Root Cause**: Fixes the fundamental off-by-one error in all [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocations, not just one.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Only modifies the numeric constants in boundary checks, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreducing risk of introducing new bugs.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistent Pattern**: Applies the same fix pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincrement check value by [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to all vulnerable locations.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Resolves ASAN Crash**: Specifically fixes line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m, which is where the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer detected the overflow.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **No Functional Changes**: The parsing logic, data structures, and algorithms [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain completely unchanged.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Same Error Detection**: The code still detects and reports the same types of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed JSON inputs; it just does so before attempting to read beyond buffer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundaries.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Backward Compatible**: Valid JSON inputs will parse identically. Only [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed inputs near buffer boundaries will be rejected earlier [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich is the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect behavior[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fixes the [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte Overflow**: The ASAN report showed a read at [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x5020000000bd[0m[39m`, which is [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m13[0m[39m-byte region. This occurs because the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` allows exactly [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m bytes to remain, but [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m pre-increments [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill read the byte at position `end`. Changing to `< [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m` prevents this.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Prevents Future Overflows**: Fixes all five instances of the same [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability pattern, preventing similar crashes with different input patterns.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Security**: Properly rejects malformed JSON at buffer boundaries [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of reading unallocated memory.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Earlier Rejection of Truncated Input**: Malformed JSON that was previously [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcausing crashes will now be rejected with error messages. This is the desired [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Performance Impact**: Changing comparison constants has negligible [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformance cost.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: The parser still accepts all valid JSON. Only [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid/truncated JSON near buffer ends is affected.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLine [0m[1;36m462[0m[39m shows the correct pattern for boundary checking:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb == [0m[32m'*'[0m[39m && state.ptr < [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && state.ptr [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m'/'[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis checks `state.ptr < [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before accessing `state.ptr [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mequivalent to checking that there's space to access the next position. Our fix [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplies the same principle: for N accesses ahead, ensure there's space for N [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpositions.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
